Defined_text = {
	name = LinkFood1Bought
	text = {
		localisation_key = "[GetLink1_prod1_bought_0to249]"
		trigger = {
			check_key = { lhs = 1_bought1 value = 0 }
			NOT = { check_key = { lhs = 1_bought1 value = 249.1 } }
		}
	}
	text = {
